[26/08/24, 10:18:12â€¯PM] NSUT Laksh Agarwal CSAI 2: ### **Thevenin's Theorem Practical - Electrical Lab**

**Objective**:  
To verify **Thevenin's Theorem** by determining Theveninâ€™s equivalent circuit of a given linear electrical network and comparing the results obtained using actual measurements and theoretical calculations.

---

#### **Apparatus Required**:

1. DC Power Supply
2. Resistors (with known resistance values)
3. Digital Multimeter (DMM)
4. Connecting Wires
5. Breadboard (optional)
6. Rheostat or Variable Resistor (optional)

---

#### **Theory**:

**Thevenin's Theorem** states that any linear electrical network with resistances and voltage sources can be replaced by a single voltage source (\( V_{th} \)) in series with a single resistance (\( R_{th} \)). The theorem simplifies complex networks into simpler two-terminal circuits, which can help in analyzing load conditions.

**Steps to apply Theveninâ€™s Theorem**:
1. **Remove the Load Resistor**: Identify and remove the load resistor where you wish to apply Theveninâ€™s Theorem.
2. **Find \( V_{th} \) (Thevenin Voltage)**: Calculate the open-circuit voltage across the terminals where the load resistor was connected.
3. **Find \( R_{th} \) (Thevenin Resistance)**:

[08/11/24, 2:59:05â€¯PM] ~â€¯SRISHTI: Greetings NSUT students!

We're pleased to open applications at the *Netaji Subhas University of Technology, Delhi* for the *Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program*, a program that helps you gain work experience in *data-driven decision-making*. 

*Benefits* post completion: 
* *Certificate of Work Experience*
* *Letter of Recommendation*
* *Certificate of Power BI Proficiency*

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba_application?src=nsutbaw

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras, and BITS Pilani* among others. 

*No pre-requisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of the project and all necessary *training* on data-driven decision-making & *Power BI* will be imparted on the project.

The project will also have *live sessions* to cover additional business cases. 

*Project Duration*: 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

The project uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading firms like *Accenture*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

*Project Start*: Flexible on student choice. It can be started *post-exams*. 

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 1999 + GST / 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *15 - 25% fee waiver* shall be given to *Netaji Subhas University of Technology, Delhi* students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1690 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST. 

The *application* process would take *2-3 mins* of your time. 

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

*Project Duration*: 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

The project uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading firms like *Accenture*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

*Project Start*: Flexible on student choice. It can be started *post-exams*. 

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 1999 + GST / 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *15 - 25% fee waiver* shall be given to *Netaji Subhas University of Technology, Delhi* students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1690 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST. 

The *application* process would take *2-3 mins* of your time. 

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

We're happy to open applications at the *Netaji Subhas University of Technology, Delhi* for the *Finlatics Machine Learning program*, an online *live project* that helps students *learn and gain experience* in *using machine learning algorithms*.

*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge are required to participate in the program. The program will impart all necessary *training* on *python and machine learning techniques*.

*Benefits* Post Completion :
1. *Certificate of Proficiency* in *Machine Learning*
2. *Letter of Recommendation* 

To apply, please use the link below:

https://www.finlatics.com/ml_application?src=nsutw

*Project Duration:* 1 month / 2 months (3-4 hours per week)

The program runs at leading institutes including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras,* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

*Project start & breaks:* *Flexible* on student choice. Can be started *post-exams*. Students can also *take a break or extension* from the program in case they need it for exams or assignments. 

If selected, the project has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 2999 + GST.

*Fee Waiver:*  A *30% fee waiver* shall be given to all *Netaji Subhas University of Technology, Delhi* students on the above mentioned minimal induction fee.

*No payment* has to be made right now

The *application* process would take *2-3 mins* of your time.

[15/01/25, 9:19:10â€¯PM] ~â€¯Vinayak Mittal: To simplify the Boolean expression A.B + A' Â· C + B Â· C, follow these steps:

Expression:  

    A.B + A' Â· C + B Â· C


Step 1: Apply the Consensus Theorem  
The Consensus Theorem states that:  

    A Â· B + A' Â· C + B Â· C = A Â· B + A' Â· C


In this case, B Â· C is the consensus term. Thus, we can eliminate B Â· C because it is already covered by A Â· B + A' Â· C.

Result:
The simplified expression is:

    A Â· B + A' Â· C


Final Answer:

    A.B + A' Â· C

NSUT Delhi Senior Professors not paid Salaries 

The NSUT has not paid the due salary to its two very senior professors who have been teaching there like a full time teacher as Emeritus Professors in department of Physics. Two Emeritus Professors namely Prof. Shatendra Kumar Sharma and Prof. Nand Lal Singh who have retired from JNU and MS University Vadodara had joined NSUT as Emeritus Professor in 2023 and 2022 respectively.  As per the terms of their appointment as Emeritus Professor, they were appointed for 3 years or 70 years of age whichever is earlier.  After the completion of 1st year of term the University issued no extension / termination orders. However, they were told that the case for extension is in process and were told to continue teaching all the courses like a regular full time faculty members of the university.  Even when the second semester started in July 2024 (that too had ended in December 2024), they continued to teach and were assured that their salary shall be released.  But till date 
1.	Professor SK Sharma has not got his salary from February 2024 onwards  (more than 11  months)
And
2.	Prof Nand Lal Singh has not got his salary from July 2024 onwards,   (about 6 months)
Despite this, they continued to teach and do all academic teaching, evaluation and research work in the interest of a students. They have written several letters and reminders to the Vice-Chancellor/HOD and Registrar etc. but no reply is ever given by the university administration neither their salaries are paid. 
The admin and HOD physics have been giving verbal assurance that the case of extension and salary is in process by the university administration. However, until July 2024 VC decided nothing. It is learnt that VC held a meeting in this connection in mid July 2024 and AR (admin) and HOD assured us that soon orders would be issued.  However, VC took no decision, not even the minutes of the meeting were finalized until October 28. 2028. NSUT administration continued to misinform us that the case is in process and orders will be issued soon. 
However,  to their surprise both Professors were given letters dated October 28th by hand on October 30th 2024 that their term shall be over on 31 Dec. 2024 with a newly carved  designation as Visiting faculty (in level of Professor)  for which they did not ever applied nor gave their consents. 

Changing the designation of two Emeritus Professors to that of visiting faculty (at the level of Professor) during their tenure is arbitrary and illegal as none of them ever submitted any application for the same. 
Both the Emeritus professors have refused to accept the new designation of visiting faculty. Because the term visiting faculty is applicable to those teachers who are already in service and not retired ones, whereas the word Emeritus means retired as per dictionary or â€œavkash praptâ€ in Hindi. However, the vice-chancellor and the administration had not responded to several letters and recommendations sent by the head of department of Physics the letters written by both professors.  Since March 24, 2024 Professor Shatendra Sharma has written several letters to the Vice-Chancellor and reminders thereafter but no reply is ever been given and neither the request to meet the Vice Chancellor has been accepted as he does not want to see any faculty member.

The delayed and arbitrary decision on extension of tenure issue of Emeritus Professors from February 2024 to October 28, 2024 smells the malefic and intentional by the NSUT Vice-Chancellor. There seems to be a total policy paralysis at NSUT and it is heading towards an administrative collapse.

It may be noted that 
â€¢	It is illegal to change the nomenclature during the tenure of service.
â€¢	It is illegal to offer a designation to the applicants for which they have not applied
â€¢	It is illegal  and unlawful to withhold the salary of any employee 
â€¢	It is against basic etiquette by and office not to reply  or respond to the grievances of faculty
â€¢	It is administrative failure if VC does not meets its staff and faculty.
â€¢	It is a collapse of administration if decisions are not taken in reasonable time
â€¢	It is an academic cheating/dishonesty by a VC to show the work of his predecessor as his to LG
